msg:My baby is 15 and a half months old. Since she was 6 months old, she has been traveling with her. She has stayed in five-star hotels, state guesthouses, and chain five-star hotels. This hotel is currently the most unsuitable for children. The hotel that gave me the worst impression and will definitely not stay again!
First of all, let's talk about a little bit, that is, the front desk, concierge, room cleaning, and service are all very good! The surrounding environment of the hotel is definitely good, very close to Little Putuo!
Next is the disadvantage, and also for families with small children, it must not be accommodated! It's a health issue!
First: the crib is very hard. There is no mattress at all. It is just a thin quilt, covered on a wooden board. The bottom board is still a kind of *****. If you sleep directly, the child will definitely not be able to eat it. Fortunately, we are driving by ourselves Bring a bed-in-bed and put it in a crib. When I brought this bed, there was still a lot of hair on the bed, and I rolled it myself with a roller!
The second is what shocked and scared me the most! In the Children's Paradise of the Cultural and Sports Building, when my daughter was crawling on the floor mat, she found a bug that resembled a centipede! After my husband saw it, he immediately took the baby and left there! At first I thought it should be fine and I didn't get bitten, because when the bug was found, it was already dead, but when I got home at night, when I was bathing the child, I found that her back and shoulders had been bitten a lot, and they were all red and swollen. ! To be honest, my daughter has grown to 15 months and has been traveling with her and staying in hotels, but! Add up the bitten mosquito blocks, no more than three! When I saw it, I was very distressed!
Third, we stayed for two nights. My baby usually wakes up very late. She doesn't wake up until ten o'clock. On the first morning, she wakes up earlier, and wakes up before nine o'clock. We will wake up as soon as possible. Take her to the restaurant for breakfast. But the next day, she woke up relatively late. I arrived at the restaurant a little after 9 o'clock. After arriving at the restaurant, I helped my husband to get some food. I wanted to ask the restaurant for a packing box and bring some to my husband to eat, because the child was there. Sleeping, it is impossible to wake her up, go to breakfast together, or leave her alone in the room, the two of us go to breakfast together! But unexpectedly, such a simple request was rejected by the restaurant foreman on the same day. I explained the situation to him, but he still disagreed, and I didn't talk to him. But the hotel I stayed in before, if I encountered such a situation, after I explained it to the hotel, it would give me two packing boxes and let me pack a little and take it back to the room! Because we originally had two breakfasts, and we had a baby, it was only a special case! In other state guests, or chain five-star hotels, they have never rejected me!
Fourth, after I booked on Ctrip, I called the front desk of the hotel and told them that I wanted to reserve a baby cot and a non-smoking room, but they told me that their hotel did not have a non-smoking room, but they could ask the cleaners to check in when we checked in. Open the balcony door for ventilation. I was also surprised by this at the time, no matter whether the state guest or the chain, there will be non-smoking rooms. But because the reservations made on Ctrip cannot be refunded or changed, so forget about it, because I really did not expect that there are no non-smoking rooms in five-star hotels now! On the first day, we arrived at about seven o'clock in the evening. When we got to the room, there was a very bad smell, which was straight into the nose. It was the smell of smoke that has been around for years, and the smell of sewage mixed together! I immediately called the front desk, asked to change rooms, and changed my room in time, but it still smelled, a little better than the previous one. Because it was late, we didn't eat, and even if it was, we didn't ask for a change.
Fifth, after a little tidying up in the room, we came to Man Tingfang, the Chinese restaurant of the hotel. We arrived at the restaurant at about 7:30. We sat down and it didn't take a while, because I helped the child sterilize the baby chair. Order immediately, the waiter, came and told us, let's order as soon as possible, said the chef will be off work at 9! My God, which restaurant chef leaves work at 9 o'clock? We ordered as soon as possible, because we also wanted to go back to the room earlier, wash the child, and let her go to bed earlier. But getting off work at 9 o'clock is really speechless!
